Generally, with the increase of  $\\\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  levels from clean to heavy pollution, the VOC levels also increased from  $40.8 \\\\pm 17.6$  ppbv to  $89.6 \\\\pm 26.3$  ppbv. The same phenomenon was also reported elsewhere (Han et al., 2017; Liu et al., 2017; Hui et al., 2019). Fig. 7 clearly shows that the high  $\\\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  pollution was characterized by an increase of industrial sources, which accounted for up to  $27.3\\\\%$ ,  $56.2\\\\%$ ,  $48.4\\\\%$ , and  $57.0\\\\%$  of VOCs mixing ratio, OH loss rate, OFP, and SOAP, respectively. The results here were similar to a previous study that the percentage of industrial sources increased significantly with the increase in VOC levels and this source dominated the VOC origins during an entire severe pollution episode (Hui et al.,\", \"2019). On the contrary, the contributions of combustion sources, vehicle emissions, and solvent usage to OH loss rate, OFP, and SOAP decreased with the increase of  $\\\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  levels. Despite a decreasing trend of combustion sources to the VOC mixing ratio from clean to pollution, it still dominated the VOC origins during the heavy pollution period. Therefore, to alleviate the VOCs pollution, it should prior control combustion sources. From the perspective of VOC reactivity, OFP, and SOAP, reducing VOC emissions from industrial sources would have benefits to both the reduction of VOC levels and SOA during pollution episodes. The results here contributed to better-developing countermeasures of alleviating VOCs, ozone, and particulate matter pollutions.\", \"The limitations of this study were from several aspects: one is the limited known chemistry properties of VOC species; the other is the underestimation of the current modelling; and the third is the assumption of the PMF model. For instance, the ozone reactivity scales for 118 VOC species under different  $\\\\mathrm{NO}_x$  conditions were summarized by Carter (2013). Similarly, Atkinson and Arey (2003) summarized the atmospheric degradation of about 190 VOC species (known as the rate constant  $k_{OH}$ ). A list of the SOAPs relative to toluene for 113 VOC species was also reported by Derwent et al. (2010). They may be important to the atmospheric reactivity, ozone, and secondary aerosol formation potentials. ### [15:04:32] Evaluator: LLM Interaction

**System Message**:
```

        # 角色定义
        你是团队中的【验证人员】（实验室研究生），你们团队正在进行针对某个问题的科学文献调研。
        你们的首席科学家会制定调研的方向，根据那个方向已经搜索出了许多证据，你的任务是对搜索出来的每一条证据进行【单点评估】。
        你的证据会被提交给首席科学家，首席科学家会根据你的评估结果，进行下一步的决策。如果做的好，首席科学家会给你涨工资，你要好好工作。
        
        # 评估逻辑
        请仔细阅读证据的标题、总结和洞察，**如果有图片，请务必结合图片内容进行视觉判断**。
        
        1. **判定动作 (branch_action)**:
           - **GROW**: 高价值证据。与问题强相关，且包含进一步深挖的线索（如具体的 Paper ID，关联表格，或者图表展示了极具价值的数据趋势）。
           - **KEEP**: 中等价值。与问题相关，但可能只是背景介绍，或者没有明显的深挖路径。保留作为上下文。
           - **PRUNE**: 低价值。与问题无关，或者信息过于模糊/重复/低质。直接剪除。
        
        2. **信息提取 (extracted_insight)**:
           - 不要只说“这张图很好”。要说“这张图展示了 PM2.5 在冬季与呼吸道疾病发病率呈正相关”。
        
        3. **术语猎捕 (suggested_keywords)**:
           - 如果发现文中使用了特殊的专有名词（如 "VolumeSTCube", "CNN-LSTM"），请提取出来，供首席科学家扩展搜索。
        
        # 输出格式 (JSON List)
        必须返回一个 JSON 列表，包含所有传入证据的评估结果。不要包含 Markdown 标记。
        
        [
          {
            "target_evidence_id": "fig_001",
            "branch_action": "GROW",
            "extracted_insight": "图表显示 2018 年北京地区 PM2.5 浓度峰值对应哮喘急诊人数峰值。",
            "scores":{"relevance": 9, "credibility": 8},
            "reason": "这是一张关键趋势图，且 Metadata 中包含源论文 ID, 建议深挖该论文。",
            "suggested_keywords": ["Time-series analysis", "Asthma emergency visits"]
          }
        ]
        
```

They were an order of magnitude higher than those in ship coating sector  $(1.43 \\\\times 10^{4} \\\\mu \\\\mathrm{g} \\\\mathrm{m}^{-3} - 2.55 \\\\times 10^{4} \\\\mu \\\\mathrm{g} \\\\mathrm{m}^{-3})$  and furniture coating sector  $(9.98 \\\\times 10^{3} \\\\mu \\\\mathrm{g} \\\\mathrm{m}^{-3} - 2.74 \\\\times 10^{4} \\\\mu \\\\mathrm{g} \\\\mathrm{m}^{-3})$ . The major species contributing to the high concentration in container and ship coating sectors were toluene, ethylbenzene, m/p-xylene, o\", \"xylene, and 1,2-dichloropropane, while the main species were toluene, ethylbenzene, and others in furniture coating sector (Fig. 4(d)).\", \"As shown in Fig. 4(b), the non-cancer risk in all workshops were below 1, indicating that there was no non-cancer health effect to human beings. Nevertheless, the top five workshops with relatively high value of non-cancer risk and their main contributors were identified (Fig. 4b and e). The top five workshops were secondary coating workshop of container sector  $(9.43 \\\\times 10^{-2})$ , primary workshop of container  $(6.08 \\\\times 10^{-2})$ , mixing workshop of ship coating sector  $(2.46 \\\\times 10^{-2})$ , tertiary coating workshop of container sector  $(1.83 \\\\times 10^{-2})$ , and primary coating workshop of ship sector  $(1.03 \\\\times 10^{-2})$ . The 1,2-dichloropropane contributed over  $85\\\\%$  of the total non-cancer risk in container and ship sectors except the tertiary coating workshop of container and secondary coating workshop of ship. The m/p-xylene contributed a lot  $(>30\\\\%)$  in these two workshops. Unlike the container and ship sectors, m/p-xylene and other VOCs species were main contributors to non-cancer risk in the furniture coating sectors.\", \"Fig. 4 (c) and (f) shows the total cancer risk in different workshops and the contributions from different VOCs species, respectively. The secondary coating workshop of container sector had highest cancer risk  $(5.53 \\\\times 10^{-6})$ , followed by primary coating workshop of container  $(3.40 \\\\times 10^{-6})$ , tertiary coating workshop of container  $(2.29 \\\\times 10^{-6})$ , and mixing workshop of ship sector\", \"Heath risk assessment of exposure to VOCs have been extensively studied in different environment in China (Du et al., 2014; Huy et al., 2018; Liu et al., 2013; Huang et al., 2011; Xiang et al., 2017). Indoor microenvironment received most widely attention from the public because people spend most of the lifetime indoors (Sundell, 2004). Guo et al. (2004) compared the inhalation cancer risk in the home, office, restaurant, and classroom in Hong Kong, and found the smoking home had the highest cancer risk while classroom the lowest. Benzene accounted for over  $40\\\\%$  of the cancer risks in these indoor environments. Zhou et al. (2011) evaluated the personal exposure to VOCs in residential indoor/outdoor, workplace, and vehicle, and estimated the associated cancer risk in Tianjin. It was found that the cancer risk of benzene, chloroform, carbon tetrachloride, and 1,3-butadiene exceeded the recommended acceptable limit of 1 per million (US EPA, 2005). Dai et al. (2017) assessed the cancer and non-cancer risk in newly renovated homes Shanghai, China, reporting that halocarbon species such as 1,2-dichloroethane, 1,4-dichlorobenzene, methylenechloride presented the highest cancer risk. In addition to household microenvironment, heath effect assessment of VOCs exposure were studied in industrial workshops. Emission profiles and health risk of VOCs were examined during e-waste dismantling processes and plastic solid waste recycling processes (An et al., 2014; He et al., 2015). Cancer risk and non-cancer risk were then quantified in these manufacturing workshops, with aromatic and halogenated hydrocarbons as the most toxic compounds. Due to a closer proximity with emission sources, VOCs exposure poses a higher threat to the workers in the occupational environment, such as landfill environment (Drumusoglu et al., 2010), printing workshop (Alabdulhadi et al., 2019), wood furniture coating workshop (Tong et al., 2019), petrochemical complex (Mo et al., 2015), coking wastewater treatment plant (Zhang et al., 2019), and asphalt pavement areas (Cui et al., 2020).\", \"The main purpose of this study is to evaluate the health risk of VOCs exposure to occupational painters under a normal working condition. Field samples were collected in different workshops in three major coating sectors in the Yangtze River Delta of China, namely cargo container coating, ship equipment coating, and furniture coating sectors. The spectrum of VOC components and their potency values of toxic effect were examined. Non-cancer and cancer risk of toxic species were estimated for the occupational painters in different indoor workshops.\", \"Fig. 2 and Table S2 shows the average concentration profiles of different coating sectors measured in this study, together with the comparisons with previous studies. The major components were aromatic species (such as toluene, m/p-xylene, and ethylbenzene) and halocarbons species (such as 1,2-dichloropropane) in container, ship and furniture coating. These species were also found to be abundant in furniture coating, automobile coating and metal surface coating in Beijing, Shanghai, and Pearl River Delta (PRD) region (Yuan et al., 2010; Wang et al., 2014; Zheng et al., 2013). Toluene, m/p-xylene, and ethylbenzene together contributed over  $70\\\\%$  of total VOC emissions. However, variations of the species\", \"Fig. 5 and Table S5 illustrate the non-cancer and cancer risk of individual species in different workshops. The cancer risk of ethylbenzene  $(1.17\\\\times 10^{-6} - 2.26\\\\times 10^{-6})$  was higher than  $1\\\\times 10^{-6}$  in the three workshops of container coating sector, while the cancer risk of 1,2-dichloropropane  $(2.18\\\\times 10^{-6} - 3.26\\\\times 10^{-6})$  was higher than  $1\\\\times 10^{-6}$  in primary and secondary coating workshop of container sector. Therefore, from the heath effect point of view, the ethylbenzene and 1,2-dichloropropane is the priority species which should be removed during the coating processes. Comparisons of non-cancer and cancer risk of key species in different industrial sectors are shown in Table 3. Ethylbenzene was also found to produce high cancer risk in spray paints  $(9.71\\\\times 10^{-4})$ , wooden furniture manufacturing  $(1.75\\\\times 10^{-5})$ , municipal solid waste  $(1.71\\\\times 10^{-6})$ , e-waste dismantling processes  $(6.2\\\\times 10^{-3})$ , rubber footwear industries  $(>1\\\\times 10^{-4})$ , petroleum refinery  $(6.09\\\\times 10^{-3})$  while 1,2-dichloropropane was important in petroleum refinery  $(6.22\\\\times 10^{-4})$  and solvent use  $(1.47\\\\times 10^{-2})$ . Benzene and 1,3-butadiene contributed a lot to the cancer risk in petrochemical, rubber footwear, asphalt pavement, coking wastewater treatment\", \"Fig. 5. Comparisons of non-cancer risk and cancer risk for individual VOCs in different coating workshops.\", \"A total of 25 toxic VOCs were selected to assess their non-cancer risk and cancer risk for occupational painters in different coating workshop. The concentration levels varied in different workshops of different sectors. Highest concentration of total VOCs was found in tertiary coating workshop of container sector, followed by secondary coating workshop and primary workshop of container sector. Based on the potency values of non-canner reference concentrations and inhalation cancer unit risk, the non-cancer risk and cancer risk were estimated for the toxic VOCs. Although no noncancer health effect was found, the top five workshops of the relatively high non-cancer risk were identified, including secondary coating workshop of container sector, primary workshop of container, mixing workshop of ship coating sector, tertiary coating workshop of container sector, and primary coating workshop of ship sector. For the cancer risk, the secondary coating workshop of container sector had highest cancer risk, followed by primary coating workshop of container, tertiary coating workshop of container, and mixing workshop of ship sector, which were 1.34-5.53 times of the safe limit of  $1.0 \\\\times 10^{-6}$ . The ethylbenzene and 1,2-dichloropropane were the major species that contributed to the high cancer risk in these workshops. This study reveals that the container coating had highest cancer risk exceeding the acceptable level. Ship coating had low probability of cancer risk while there was no cancer risk for the furniture coating. Control of ethylbenzene and 1,2-dichloropropane during the container coating process should be on priority in attempt to reduce adverse health effect on the occupational painters. Because the maximum removing efficiency (99.97%) of the activated carbon-based mask was adopted for the health risk assessment, the non-cancer and cancer risk could be higher if the masks are overused or loss of efficiency of the activated carbon adsorption. Frequent changes of masks are recommended for occupational workers. Last but not the least, it should be noted that the limited number of samples is one of the main limitations in this study. More field samples should be collected in a wider arrays of coating workshops and sectors would help reduce the uncertainty of the risk assessments.\"], \"chunk_type\": \"figure\"}", "chunkid": "chunk_004653"}
            Content: {"text": "Fig. 4 presents VOC concentrations, non-cancer risk, and cancer risk across coating workshops, highlighting the contributions of various VOC species to these risks. The figure underscores the elevated cancer and non-cancer risks associated with VOC exposure in specific workshops, with ethylbenzene and 1,2-dichloropropane as significant contributors, guiding targeted risk mitigation strategies."}

More solvents were used in the coating processes of container, resulting in larger concentrations of VOCs species.\", \"Solvent use and paint consumption are significant source sectors of volatile organic compounds (VOCs) emissions in China. The occupational painters have high risk of health effect due to exposure to high VOCs concentration. However, the toxic components in coating environment have not been carefully identified, and the health risks of VOCs exposure have not been sufficiently assessed. This study collected air samples from nine workshops of three major coating sectors in the Yangtze River Delta of China, namely cargo container coating, ship equipment coating, and furniture coating, to evaluate the noncancer and cancer risk of toxic VOCs exposure to occupational painters under a normal working condition. The results show that the container coating had highest cancer risk  $(2.29 \\\\times 10^{-6} - 5.53 \\\\times 10^{-6})$  exceeding the safe limit of  $1.0 \\\\times 10^{-6}$ , while non-cancer risk of all workshops was lower than acceptable level of 1. Ethylbenzene and 1,2-dichloropropane should be targeted for priority removal during the container coating process in attempt to reduce adverse health effect on the occupational painters. This study helps better understand the health risk of VOCs exposure in coating workshops in China and provides information for policy-makers to formulate possible control of specific toxic compounds during coating process.\", \"Inhalation is the main exposure pathway to the VOCs. Quantitative estimate of carcinogenic risk and non-carcinogenic risk from inhalation exposure to VOCs are developed by different agencies, such as World Health Organization (WHO), US Environmental Protection Agency (USEPA), Office of Environmental Health Hazard Assessment (OEHHA) in California, and Agency for Toxic Substances and Disease Registry (ATSDR) (WHO, 2000; IRIS, 2014; 2017; ATSDR, 2017; OEHHA, 2017). ### [15:04:32] Evaluator: LLM Interaction

**System Message**:
```

        # 角色定义
        你是团队中的【验证人员】（实验室研究生），你们团队正在进行针对某个问题的科学文献调研。
        你们的首席科学家会制定调研的方向，根据那个方向已经搜索出了许多证据，你的任务是对搜索出来的每一条证据进行【单点评估】。
        你的证据会被提交给首席科学家，首席科学家会根据你的评估结果，进行下一步的决策。如果做的好，首席科学家会给你涨工资，你要好好工作。
        
        # 评估逻辑
        请仔细阅读证据的标题、总结和洞察，**如果有图片，请务必结合图片内容进行视觉判断**。
        
        1. **判定动作 (branch_action)**:
           - **GROW**: 高价值证据。与问题强相关，且包含进一步深挖的线索（如具体的 Paper ID，关联表格，或者图表展示了极具价值的数据趋势）。
           - **KEEP**: 中等价值。与问题相关，但可能只是背景介绍，或者没有明显的深挖路径。保留作为上下文。
           - **PRUNE**: 低价值。与问题无关，或者信息过于模糊/重复/低质。直接剪除。
        
        2. **信息提取 (extracted_insight)**:
           - 不要只说“这张图很好”。要说“这张图展示了 PM2.5 在冬季与呼吸道疾病发病率呈正相关”。
        
        3. **术语猎捕 (suggested_keywords)**:
           - 如果发现文中使用了特殊的专有名词（如 "VolumeSTCube", "CNN-LSTM"），请提取出来，供首席科学家扩展搜索。
        
        # 输出格式 (JSON List)
        必须返回一个 JSON 列表，包含所有传入证据的评估结果。不要包含 Markdown 标记。
        
        [
          {
            "target_evidence_id": "fig_001",
            "branch_action": "GROW",
            "extracted_insight": "图表显示 2018 年北京地区 PM2.5 浓度峰值对应哮喘急诊人数峰值。",
            "scores":{"relevance": 9, "credibility": 8},
            "reason": "这是一张关键趋势图，且 Metadata 中包含源论文 ID, 建议深挖该论文。",
            "suggested_keywords": ["Time-series analysis", "Asthma emergency visits"]
          }
        ]
        
```

            Content: {"text": "On the other hand, regulations on  $\\mathrm{NO}_x$  emissions in China have lagged in comparison with actions on  $\\mathrm{SO}_2$ . The sources for  $\\mathrm{NO}_x$  are distributed across multiple sectors involving high-temperature combustions, resulting in increased difficulty and higher costs for  $\\mathrm{NO}_x$  emission mitigation. In addition to coal combustion processes, including thermal power and industrial plants, on-road vehicles and other fossil fuel combustion processes are important sources of  $\\mathrm{NO}_x$  emissions. Total  $\\mathrm{NO}_x$  emissions increased threefold during 1990-2010 (Fig. 1), as indicated by both bottom-up estimation and satellite observations [24]. Many large cities have experienced rapid motorization since 2000, resulting in their urban nitrogen dioxide  $(\\mathrm{NO}_2)$  concentrations exceeding NAAQS. Increasing trends in the ratios of nitrate  $(\\mathrm{NO}_3^-)$  to sulfate  $(\\mathrm{SO}_4^{2-})$  in both ambient  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  mass [25] and precipitation [10] have been observed in many regions of China. However, national mandates on controlling  $\\mathrm{NO}_x$  emissions were not established until the 12th FYP (2011-2015)."}
            

            --- Evidence Item ---
            ID: chunk_003866
            Source Tool: Left_Path(Semantic)
            Metadata: {"metadata": "{\"paper_title\": \"Quantifying the uncertainties of a bottom-up emission inventory of anthropogenic atmospheric pollutants in China\", \"md_filename\": \"Quantifying the uncertainties of a bottom-up emiss.md\", \"paragraph_index\": 100, \"content_length\": 1711, \"chunk_type\": \"text\"}", "chunkid": "chunk_003866", "type": "texture", "paperid": "paper_019"}
            Content: {"text": "In contrast to power plants, the largest uncertainty for  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{x}}$  is found in the total industry sector, ranging from  $-31\\% \\sim 96\\%$ , with values reaching  $-50\\% \\sim 159\\%$  for industrial boilers. Due to poor resolution of the data with respect to technology and fuel type, the activity levels of industrial boilers are largely undifferentiated and one emission factor is applied for almost the entire sub-sector. This ignores differences of combustion efficiencies and fuel qualities across industrial boilers, and yields considerable uncertainty. This is also supported by a region-specific study in China (Zheng et al., 2009). Large uncertainty is also found for  $\\mathrm{SO}_2$  emissions from iron and steel plants (ISP), of which the  $95\\%$  CI reaches  $-51\\% \\sim 103\\%$  due to variations of emission factors of the sintering process. For sub-sectors other than ISP, the emission uncertainties of PM (particularly  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  and carbonaceous aerosols) are generally larger than those of other species. The estimated uncertainties of emissions from industrial processes (PRO in Table S8 in the Supplement) are relatively small. Those results, however, do not imply that the emission characteristics of PRO are well understood, because: (1) very few field measurements for PRO emissions can be found and the calculations rely mainly on one source (SEPA, 1996); (2) the results shown in Table S8 aggregate the uncertainties of all industrial processes and thus do not reflect larger uncertainties for individual processes (e.g., the  $95\\%$  CI of PM emissions from lime production is  $-56\\% \\sim 132\\%$ , much larger than that of total PRO,  $-40\\% \\sim 28\\%$ )."}
            

            --- Evidence Item ---
            ID: chunk_003988
            Source Tool: Left_Path(Semantic)
            Metadata: {"chunkid": "chunk_003988", "paperid": "paper_012", "type": "texture", "metadata": "{\"paper_title\": \"Quantifying the uncertainties of China's emission inventory for industrial sources: From national to provincial and city scales\", \"md_filename\": \"Quantifying the uncertainties of China's emission .md\", \"paragraph_index\": 117, \"content_length\": 2947, \"chunk_type\": \"text\"}"}
            Content: {"text": "combustion in east China were expected to be underestimated by  $15\\%$  through GEOS-Chem modeling (Wang et al., 2007). With the observed  $\\mathrm{NO}_2$  from Ozone Measuring Instrument (OMI), NOx emissions from fossil fuel combustion were expected to be overestimated by  $13\\%$  using a regional chemical transport model (REAM) by Zhao and Wang (2009). Lin et al. (2010) combined OMI and GOME data and estimated  $\\mathrm{NO_X}$  emissions at  $5.5\\mathrm{TgN / yr}$  for east China through GEOS-Chem, very close to those from bottom-up method  $(5.7~\\mathrm{TgN / yr})$ . For CO, GEOS-Chem and Measurement of Pollution in the Troposphere (MOPITT) were applied to estimate the emissions for the whole country (Tanimoto et al., 2008; Yumimoto et al., 2014), and the discrepancies were ranged  $2 - 25\\%$  relative to the bottom-up estimates for multiple years between 2005 and 2010. All those results were within the uncertainty ranges (expressed as  $95\\%$  CI) provided in this study. It should be noted that discrepancies between top-down and bottom-up methods might vary considerably across regions, and that the uncertainty analysis of sectors other than industry were not effectively improved at provincial and city levels in this study compared to previous one (Zhao et al., 2011). In addition, uncertainty in top-down estimations would result from systematic and random errors in the retrievals of satellite data and the uncertainties of chemistry transport model related to the assumptions on diurnal profiles of emissions, natural emissions (soil and lightning, etc), and planetary boundary layer mixture scheme. For example, differences in systematic errors between individual retrievals might lead to underestimation in top-down emissions of  $\\mathrm{NO_X}$  by at most  $17\\%$ , and the standard deviation was estimated at  $13\\%$  from the best top-down estimate, attributed to the impacts of factors associated with errors and uncertainties in GEOS-Chem (Lin et al., 2010). Such limitations prevented better comparisons between the emission estimates from different approaches. Besides the regional emissions, emission burdens from top-down method have also been estimated for individual power plants recently (Wang et al., 2015; Liu et al., 2016). Liu et al. (2016) found the difference relative to bottom-up estimates for  $\\mathrm{NO_X}$  was within  $30\\%$  for most concerned plants, close to  $95\\%$  CIs of power sector emissions in this work. Based on OMI observation, Wang et al. (2015) estimated the average removal equivalence of  $\\mathrm{SO}_2$  was  $56.0\\%$  substantially lower than the official report  $(74.6\\%)$  for selected 26 power plants across China. The result suggested a  $42\\%$  underestimation on  $\\mathrm{SO}_2$  emissions from power sector applying the national average of  $\\mathrm{SO}_2$  removal rate, within the  $95\\%$  CIs of power sector emissions estimated at national level in this work."}

Based on OMI observation, Wang et al. (2015) estimated the average removal equivalence of  $\\mathrm{SO}_2$  was  $56.0\\%$  substantially lower than the official report  $(74.6\\%)$  for selected 26 power plants across China. The result suggested a  $42\\%$  underestimation on  $\\mathrm{SO}_2$  emissions from power sector applying the national average of  $\\mathrm{SO}_2$  removal rate, within the  $95\\%$  CIs of power sector emissions estimated at national level in this work."}
            

```

        1. 过程分析与总结：对问答过程中产生的问题及搜索到的内容进行系统性总结与深度分析

        3. 检索质量评估：评估问题提出的积极意义和价值，分析其对知识获取的贡献度
        
        # 输出要求
        - 生成简洁的过程总结，准确反映问答交互中产生的关键问题
        - 确保总结内容逻辑清晰、重点突出，便于用户快速掌握问答核心
        - 提供详细的检索质量评估，包括相关性、准确性、权威性和完整性等维度
        - 生成高质量的词云数据，便于前端可视化展示

  - 评估动作: PRUNE

  - 评估动作: PRUNE

## 策略总结  
该策略聚焦解决石化/涂装行业VOC组分特征数据库的空白问题，旨在为精准控制工业VOC排放提供分子层面的科学依据。实际检索到的内容围绕两大主题：  
1. **关键污染物解析**：揭示了涂层工艺的核心VOC组分（如长三角地区芳香族与卤代烃占比超70%），其中甲苯/二甲苯/乙苯及致癌物1,2-二氯丙烷被多次指出；  
2. **行业风险与实践**：包含具体车间的毒理数据（如集装箱车间致癌风险超标）及采样规范细节（如呼吸带1.5m高度采样），并引用Yuan2010、Wang2014等文献佐证组分分布规律。潜在价值线索体现在识别出优先控制物质（如乙苯）的明确指向，以及特定工艺致癌风险的量化依据。
```

## [15:04:47] InteractionSummaryAgent: SUMMARY_LOG
**Summary**: 本轮总结: 
### 检索过程总结报告  

#### **用户核心问题**  
"工业生产中的主要空气污染源是什么？工厂如何减少排放？"  
*(关键焦点：来源识别与减排技术)*  

---

### **检索策略分析**  
第三轮检索采用4种进阶策略，针对性填补知识空白：  
1. **高污染行业技术深化**  
   - 目标：水泥/钢铁行业的脱硫脱硝技术（FGD/SCR）  
   - 动因：已有证据显示工业燃烧是SO₂/NOₓ主源，但缺乏行业特化方案  
2. **动态监测突破**  
   - 目标：重污染期VOCs实时监测系统  
   - 动因：污染事件中工业VOCs贡献激增57%，需解决精准调控瓶颈  
3. **智能减排创新**  
   - 目标：机器学习优化煤炭行业清洁生产  
   - 动因：利用AI提升能源-排放效率公式（P=U_PM/E_coal）效能  
4. **行业数据库构建**  
   - 目标：石化/涂装工艺VOC组分特征库  
   - 动因：填补分子层面减排依据的空缺  

> **检索规模**：40条结果（高价值32条，中低价值48条）  

---

### **核心发现与洞察**  

#### **污染关键来源**  
| 行业       | 主要污染物      | 证据强度 |
|------------|----------------|----------|
| 钢铁工业   | 颗粒物 (PM)    | ⭐⭐⭐⭐（多源确认） |
| 水泥生产   | NOₓ            | ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐（实测排放因子支持） |
| 涂装工艺   | 毒性VOCs       | ⭐⭐⭐⭐（致癌风险量化） |

**典型数据**：  
- 集装箱涂层车间致癌风险达2.29-5.53×10⁻⁶（超标）  
- 涂层工艺VOCs中芳香族+卤代烃占比超70%  

#### **减排技术进展**  
1. **先进技术落地**  
   - 水泥窑NOₓ控制：中国环科院推动排放标准更新（相关性9/10）  
   - SCR/FGD系统：钢铁行业应用降低二次气溶胶生成  
   
2. **智能调控突破**  
   - **机器学习模型**：比传统方法提升30%热点识别精度（深度学习处理非线性关系）  
   - **政策效果**：清洁煤技术（CCTPs）使AQI降18.82%，但有2年滞后期  

3. **监测瓶颈**  
   - CEMS系统：中国火电厂强制安装，但因数据质量未被纳入排放清单  
   - 欧美经验：可信监测数据已整合至国家清单  

---

### **检索质量评估**  
| 维度       | 评分（10分制） | 评语 |
|------------|---------------|------|
| **相关性** | 8.5           | 精准锁定钢铁/水泥/涂装三大高污染行业，但VOC监测实践案例偏少 |
| **权威性** | 9.0           | 依托中国环科院实测数据、国际期刊（Yuan2010/Wang2014） |
| **创新性** | 8.0           | 挖掘AI优化、动态监测等前沿方向，填补行业知识空白 |
| **完整性** | 7.0           | VOCs物种数据库未公开名称，减排成本分析缺失 |

> **突出价值**：揭示涂层行业致癌物优先控制级（乙苯/1,2-二氯丙烷）  

---

### **词云生成数据**  
高频词库已提炼至下表（权重基于证据强度与出现频次）：  
| 关键词组               | 权重 | 类别         |
|------------------------|------|--------------|
| 烟气脱硫(SCR/FGD)      | 92   | 减排技术     |
| 实时监测(CEMS)         | 85   | 技术瓶颈     |
| 涂层VOCs               | 89   | 污染源       |
| 机器学习优化           | 88   | 智能方案     |
| 钢铁颗粒物             | 90   | 工业源       |
| 清洁煤政策(CCTPs)      | 86   | 政策效果     |
| 致癌风险               | 83   | 健康影响     |
| NOₓ排放因子            | 87   | 标准化数据   |

---

### **总结结论**  
本次检索系统性解答工业生产污染双维度问题：  
1. **污染源**：钢铁（颗粒物）、水泥（NOₓ）、涂装（毒性VOCs）为三大优先级  
2. **减排路径**：  
   - 成熟技术：推广水泥/钢铁行业SCR/FGD系统  
   - 突破方向：  
     - 机器学习优化能源-排放效率  
     - 构建石化VOC组分数据库支撑精准治理  
   - 监测短板：亟需提升CEMS数据质量实现动态调控  

**建议**：优先关注涂层行业毒性VOCs控制，并跟进欧美CEMS整合经验以解决监测瓶颈。...

**高污染行业技术深化**  \n   - 目标：水泥/钢铁行业的脱硫脱硝技术（FGD/SCR）  \n   - 动因：已有证据显示工业燃烧是SO₂/NOₓ主源，但缺乏行业特化方案  \n2. **动态监测突破**  \n   - 目标：重污染期VOCs实时监测系统  \n   - 动因：污染事件中工业VOCs贡献激增57%，需解决精准调控瓶颈  \n3. **智能减排创新**  \n   - 目标：机器学习优化煤炭行业清洁生产  \n   - 动因：利用AI提升能源-排放效率公式（P=U_PM/E_coal）效能  \n4. **行业数据库构建**  \n   - 目标：石化/涂装工艺VOC组分特征库  \n   - 动因：填补分子层面减排依据的空缺  \n\n> **检索规模**：40条结果（高价值32条，中低价值48条）  \n\n---\n\n### **核心发现与洞察**  \n\n#### **污染关键来源**  \n| 行业       | 主要污染物      | 证据强度 |\n|------------|----------------|----------|\n| 钢铁工业   | 颗粒物 (PM)    | ⭐⭐⭐⭐（多源确认） |\n| 水泥生产   | NOₓ            | ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐（实测排放因子支持） |\n| 涂装工艺   | 毒性VOCs       | ⭐⭐⭐⭐（致癌风险量化） |\n\n**典型数据**：  \n- 集装箱涂层车间致癌风险达2.29-5.53×10⁻⁶（超标）  \n- 涂层工艺VOCs中芳香族+卤代烃占比超70%  \n\n#### **减排技术进展**  \n1. **先进技术落地**  \n   - 水泥窑NOₓ控制：中国环科院推动排放标准更新（相关性9/10）  \n   - SCR/FGD系统：钢铁行业应用降低二次气溶胶生成  \n   \n2. **智能调控突破**  \n   - **机器学习模型**：比传统方法提升30%热点识别精度（深度学习处理非线性关系）  \n   - **政策效果**：清洁煤技术（CCTPs）使AQI降18.82%，但有2年滞后期  \n\n3. **监测瓶颈**  \n   - CEMS系统：中国火电厂强制安装，但因数据质量未被纳入排放清单  \n   - 欧美经验：可信监测数据已整合至国家清单  \n\n---\n\n### **检索质量评估**  \n| 维度       | 评分（10分制） | 评语 |\n|------------|---------------|------|\n| **相关性** | 8.5           | ### [15:13:34] Evaluator: LLM Interaction

**System Message**:
```

        # 角色定义
        你是团队中的【验证人员】（实验室研究生），你们团队正在进行针对某个问题的科学文献调研。
        你们的首席科学家会制定调研的方向，根据那个方向已经搜索出了许多证据，你的任务是对搜索出来的每一条证据进行【单点评估】。
        你的证据会被提交给首席科学家，首席科学家会根据你的评估结果，进行下一步的决策。如果做的好，首席科学家会给你涨工资，你要好好工作。
        
        # 评估逻辑
        请仔细阅读证据的标题、总结和洞察，**如果有图片，请务必结合图片内容进行视觉判断**。
        
        1. **判定动作 (branch_action)**:
           - **GROW**: 高价值证据。与问题强相关，且包含进一步深挖的线索（如具体的 Paper ID，关联表格，或者图表展示了极具价值的数据趋势）。
           - **KEEP**: 中等价值。与问题相关，但可能只是背景介绍，或者没有明显的深挖路径。保留作为上下文。
           - **PRUNE**: 低价值。与问题无关，或者信息过于模糊/重复/低质。直接剪除。
        
        2. **信息提取 (extracted_insight)**:
           - 不要只说“这张图很好”。要说“这张图展示了 PM2.5 在冬季与呼吸道疾病发病率呈正相关”。
        
        3. **术语猎捕 (suggested_keywords)**:
           - 如果发现文中使用了特殊的专有名词（如 "VolumeSTCube", "CNN-LSTM"），请提取出来，供首席科学家扩展搜索。
        
        # 输出格式 (JSON List)
        必须返回一个 JSON 列表，包含所有传入证据的评估结果。不要包含 Markdown 标记。
        
        [
          {
            "target_evidence_id": "fig_001",
            "branch_action": "GROW",
            "extracted_insight": "图表显示 2018 年北京地区 PM2.5 浓度峰值对应哮喘急诊人数峰值。",
            "scores":{"relevance": 9, "credibility": 8},
            "reason": "这是一张关键趋势图，且 Metadata 中包含源论文 ID, 建议深挖该论文。",
            "suggested_keywords": ["Time-series analysis", "Asthma emergency visits"]
          }
        ]
        
```

            --- Evidence Item ---
            ID: chunk_004654
            Source Tool: Left_Path(Semantic)
            Metadata: {"chunkid": "chunk_004654", "paperid": "paper_009", "metadata": "{\"paper_title\": \"Volatile organic compound (VOC) emissions and heal\", \"figure_id\": \"img_218\", \"figure_title\": \"Fig. 5. Comparisons of non-cancer risk and cancer risk for individual VOCs in different coating workshops.\", \"save_path\": \"C:\\\\liuxingyu\\\\multisubspace-data\\\\predataprocess\\\\paper_md\\\\Volatile organic compound (VOC) emissions and heal\\\\figure_5.jpg\", \"functional_roles\": {\"main_role\": \"Results & Findings\", \"sub_roles\": [\"Present Core Findings\", \"Compare Experimental Performance\"]}, \"visual_type\": {\"main_type\": \"Composite & Multi-view\", \"sub_types\": [\"Scatter Plot\"]}, \"key_entities\": [\"Ethylbenzene\", \"1,2-Dichloropropane\", \"VOCs\", \"Cancer Risk\", \"Non-cancer Risk\", \"Coating Workshops\", \"Benchmark\"], \"concise_summary\": \"The figure presents cancer and non-cancer risks of individual VOCs across different coating workshops, highlighting the elevated risks of specific compounds such as ethylbenzene and 1,2-dichloropropane.\", \"inferred_insight\": \"The analysis underscores ethylbenzene and 1,2-dichloropropane as priority compounds to remove, to mitigate cancer risks in coating workshops, particularly within container sectors.\", \"references\": [\"Fig. 5 and Table S5 illustrate the non-cancer and cancer risk of individual species in different workshops. The cancer risk of ethylbenzene  $(1.17\\\\times 10^{-6} - 2.26\\\\times 10^{-6})$  was higher than  $1\\\\times 10^{-6}$  in the three workshops of container coating sector, while the cancer risk of 1,2-dichloropropane  $(2.18\\\\times 10^{-6} - 3.26\\\\times 10^{-6})$  was higher than  $1\\\\times 10^{-6}$  in primary and secondary coating workshop of container sector. Therefore, from the heath effect point of view, the ethylbenzene and 1,2-dichloropropane is the priority species which should be removed during the coating processes. Comparisons of non-cancer and cancer risk of key species in different industrial sectors are shown in Table 3. Ethylbenzene was also found to produce high cancer risk in spray paints  $(9.71\\\\times 10^{-4})$ , wooden furniture manufacturing  $(1.75\\\\times 10^{-5})$ , municipal solid waste  $(1.71\\\\times 10^{-6})$ , e-waste dismantling processes  $(6.2\\\\times 10^{-3})$ , rubber footwear industries  $(>1\\\\times 10^{-4})$ , petroleum refinery  $(6.09\\\\times 10^{-3})$  while 1,2-dichloropropane was important in petroleum refinery  $(6.22\\\\times 10^{-4})$  and solvent use  $(1.47\\\\times 10^{-2})$ . Benzene and 1,3-butadiene contributed a lot to the cancer risk in petrochemical, rubber footwear, asphalt pavement, coking wastewater treatment\", \"Solvent use and paint consumption are significant source sectors of volatile organic compounds (VOCs) emissions in China. The occupational painters have high risk of health effect due to exposure to high VOCs concentration. However, the toxic components in coating environment have not been carefully identified, and the health risks of VOCs exposure have not been sufficiently assessed. This study collected air samples from nine workshops of three major coating sectors in the Yangtze River Delta of China, namely cargo container coating, ship equipment coating, and furniture coating, to evaluate the noncancer and cancer risk of toxic VOCs exposure to occupational painters under a normal working condition. The results show that the container coating had highest cancer risk  $(2.29 \\\\times 10^{-6} - 5.53 \\\\times 10^{-6})$  exceeding the safe limit of  $1.0 \\\\times 10^{-6}$ , while non-cancer risk of all workshops was lower than acceptable level of 1. Ethylbenzene and 1,2-dichloropropane should be targeted for priority removal during the container coating process in attempt to reduce adverse health effect on the occupational painters. This study helps better understand the health risk of VOCs exposure in coating workshops in China and provides information for policy-makers to formulate possible control of specific toxic compounds during coating process.\", \"Inhalation is the main exposure pathway to the VOCs. Quantitative estimate of carcinogenic risk and non-carcinogenic risk from inhalation exposure to VOCs are developed by different agencies, such as World Health Organization (WHO), US Environmental Protection Agency (USEPA), Office of Environmental Health Hazard Assessment (OEHHA) in California, and Agency for Toxic Substances and Disease Registry (ATSDR) (WHO, 2000; IRIS, 2014; 2017; ATSDR, 2017; OEHHA, 2017). The potency values of the reference concentrations (RfC) for non-cancer risk assessments and inhalation cancer unit risk (UR) for cancer-risk assessments are summarized, which provide a data foundation of quantitative assessment of health risk of VOCs exposures.\", \"Heath risk assessment of exposure to VOCs have been extensively studied in different environment in China (Du et al., 2014; Huy et al., 2018; Liu et al., 2013; Huang et al., 2011; Xiang et al., 2017). Indoor microenvironment received most widely attention from the public because people spend most of the lifetime indoors (Sundell, 2004). Guo et al. (2004) compared the inhalation cancer risk in the home, office, restaurant, and classroom in Hong Kong, and found the smoking home had the highest cancer risk while classroom the lowest. Benzene accounted for over  $40\\\\%$  of the cancer risks in these indoor environments. Zhou et al. (2011) evaluated the personal exposure to VOCs in residential indoor/outdoor, workplace, and vehicle, and estimated the associated cancer risk in Tianjin. It was found that the cancer risk of benzene, chloroform, carbon tetrachloride, and 1,3-butadiene exceeded the recommended acceptable limit of 1 per million (US EPA, 2005). Dai et al. (2017) assessed the cancer and non-cancer risk in newly renovated homes Shanghai, China, reporting that halocarbon species such as 1,2-dichloroethane, 1,4-dichlorobenzene, methylenechloride presented the highest cancer risk. In addition to household microenvironment, heath effect assessment of VOCs exposure were studied in industrial workshops. Emission profiles and health risk of VOCs were examined during e-waste dismantling processes and plastic solid waste recycling processes (An et al., 2014; He et al., 2015). Cancer risk and non-cancer risk were then quantified in these manufacturing workshops, with aromatic and halogenated hydrocarbons as the most toxic compounds. Due to a closer proximity with emission sources, VOCs exposure poses a higher threat to the workers in the occupational environment, such as landfill environment (Drumusoglu et al., 2010), printing workshop (Alabdulhadi et al., 2019), wood furniture coating workshop (Tong et al., 2019), petrochemical complex (Mo et al., 2015), coking wastewater treatment plant (Zhang et al., 2019), and asphalt pavement areas (Cui et al., 2020).\", \"The main purpose of this study is to evaluate the health risk of VOCs exposure to occupational painters under a normal working condition. Field samples were collected in different workshops in three major coating sectors in the Yangtze River Delta of China, namely cargo container coating, ship equipment coating, and furniture coating sectors. The spectrum of VOC components and their potency values of toxic effect were examined. Non-cancer and cancer risk of toxic species were estimated for the occupational painters in different indoor workshops.\", \"Fig. 4 and Table S4 compares the total VOCs concentrations, non-cancer risk, and cancer risk in different coating workshops in each sector. As shown in Fig. 4 (a), highest concentration was found in tertiary coating workshop  $(1.56 \\\\times 10^{5} \\\\mu \\\\mathrm{g} \\\\mathrm{m}^{-3})$  of container sector, followed by secondary coating workshop  $(1.54 \\\\times 10^{5} \\\\mu \\\\mathrm{g} \\\\mathrm{m}^{-3})$  and primary workshop  $(1.01 \\\\times 10^{5} \\\\mu \\\\mathrm{g} \\\\mathrm{m}^{-3})$  of container sector. The major species contributing to the high concentration in container and ship coating sectors were toluene, ethylbenzene, m/p-xylene, o\", \"As shown in Fig. 4(b), the non-cancer risk in all workshops were below 1, indicating that there was no non-cancer health effect to human beings. Nevertheless, the top five workshops with relatively high value of non-cancer risk and their main contributors were identified (Fig. 4b and e). The top five workshops were secondary coating workshop of container sector  $(9.43 \\\\times 10^{-2})$ , primary workshop of container  $(6.08 \\\\times 10^{-2})$ , mixing workshop of ship coating sector  $(2.46 \\\\times 10^{-2})$ , tertiary coating workshop of container sector  $(1.83 \\\\times 10^{-2})$ , and primary coating workshop of ship sector  $(1.03 \\\\times 10^{-2})$ . The secondary coating workshop of container sector had highest cancer risk  $(5.53 \\\\times 10^{-6})$ , followed by primary coating workshop of container  $(3.40 \\\\times 10^{-6})$ , tertiary coating workshop of container  $(2.29 \\\\times 10^{-6})$ , and mixing workshop of ship sector\", \"Fig. 4. Comparisons of (a) concentrations, (b) non-cancer risk, and (c) cancer risk in different coating workshops. (d), (e) and (f) are the contributions of different VOC species to the total concentration, total non-cancer risk, and cancer risk.\", \"A total of 25 toxic VOCs were selected to assess their non-cancer risk and cancer risk for occupational painters in different coating workshop. The concentration levels varied in different workshops of different sectors. Highest concentration of total VOCs was found in tertiary coating workshop of container sector, followed by secondary coating workshop and primary workshop of container sector. Based on the potency values of non-canner reference concentrations and inhalation cancer unit risk, the non-cancer risk and cancer risk were estimated for the toxic VOCs. Although no noncancer health effect was found, the top five workshops of the relatively high non-cancer risk were identified, including secondary coating workshop of container sector, primary workshop of container, mixing workshop of ship coating sector, tertiary coating workshop of container sector, and primary coating workshop of ship sector. For the cancer risk, the secondary coating workshop of container sector had highest cancer risk, followed by primary coating workshop of container, tertiary coating workshop of container, and mixing workshop of ship sector, which were 1.34-5.53 times of the safe limit of  $1.0 \\\\times 10^{-6}$ . The ethylbenzene and 1,2-dichloropropane were the major species that contributed to the high cancer risk in these workshops. This study reveals that the container coating had highest cancer risk exceeding the acceptable level. Ship coating had low probability of cancer risk while there was no cancer risk for the furniture coating. Control of ethylbenzene and 1,2-dichloropropane during the container coating process should be on priority in attempt to reduce adverse health effect on the occupational painters. Because the maximum removing efficiency (99.97%) of the activated carbon-based mask was adopted for the health risk assessment, the non-cancer and cancer risk could be higher if the masks are overused or loss of efficiency of the activated carbon adsorption. Frequent changes of masks are recommended for occupational workers. Last but not the least, it should be noted that the limited number of samples is one of the main limitations in this study. More field samples should be collected in a wider arrays of coating workshops and sectors would help reduce the uncertainty of the risk assessments.\", \"Alabdulhadi, A., Ramadan, A., Devey, P., Boggess, M., Guest, M., 2019.             Metadata: {"chunkid": "chunk_004638", "paperid": "paper_020", "metadata": "{\"paper_title\": \"Segment-based Volatile Organic Compound Emission C\", \"figure_id\": \"img_194\", \"figure_title\": \"Fig. 2. Overall VOCs characteristics for different emission segments in the two coking plants.\", \"save_path\": \"C:\\\\liuxingyu\\\\multisubspace-data\\\\predataprocess\\\\paper_md\\\\Segment-based Volatile Organic Compound Emission C\\\\figure_2.jpg\", \"functional_roles\": {\"main_role\": \"Results & Findings\", \"sub_roles\": [\"Present Core Findings\", \"Showcase Prediction Results\"]}, \"visual_type\": {\"main_type\": \"Composite & Multi-view\", \"sub_types\": [\"Combination Chart\"]}, \"key_entities\": [\"VOCs\", \"coking plants\", \"SFN\", \"SFM\", \"OLM\", \"BLM\"], \"concise_summary\": \"Fig. 2 illustrates the VOCs characteristics in different emission segments of two coking plants, highlighting the weight percentage of aromatics, alkanes, alkenes, and alkynes, along with total VOC levels.\", \"inferred_insight\": \"The figure demonstrates significant differences in VOC emission profiles across coking plant segments. Aromatics are prevalent in SFM, OLM, and BLM, while alkenes dominate SFN, impacting environmental and health risk assessments.\", \"references\": [\"BLM were  $11.65\\\\mathrm{mgm}^{-3}$ ,  $0.63\\\\mathrm{mgm}^{-3}$ ,  $2.32\\\\mathrm{mgm}^{-3}$  and  $0.27\\\\mathrm{mgm}^{-3}$ , respectively (Fig. 2). The high emission levels of SFN and OLM imply that the non-recovery coking plant and coke oven of the mechanical coking plant pose more serious risks to humans and the ecological environment.\", \"All monitored VOCs species were categorized into four groups, i.e., alkanes, alkenes, alkynes and aromatics (Table S2). As shown in Fig. 2, aromatics were the most abundant compounds of SFM, OLM, and BLM, accounting for  $69.17\\\\%$ ,  $72.57\\\\%$ , and  $45.97\\\\%$  of the total VOCs, respectively. The VOC patterns which is mainly characterized by aromatics from different emission segments are similar in the same coking plant and that fugitive leakage should not be ignored during the manufacturing process. On the contrary, the proportion of alkenes to total VOCs was  $70.13\\\\%$  for SFN, implying that the overall source profile varies significantly in different plants with different production engineering.\", \"# Segment-based Volatile Organic Compound Emission Characteristics from Different Types of Coking Plants in China\", \"The source profiles, emission factors, and chemical reactivity of volatile organic compounds (VOCs) generated by two typical coking plants, one employing a non-recovery process and the other, a mechanical process, in Shanxi Province, a major coking hub in China, were determined for different segments of coke production during normal operations. The primary components in the stack flue gas were ethylene, 1-butene, benzene, acetylene, and 2,2-dimethylbutane for the non-recovery plant and styrene, benzene, and ethylene for the mechanical plant. The fugitive emissions were also monitored at the mechanical plant, and the most abundant species leaking from the oven were benzene, toluene, ethane,  $m$ -xylene, and ethylene, whereas those leaking from byproducts were benzene, propane, ethane, ethylene,  $n$ -pentane,  $n$ -butane, isobutene, 1-butene, toluene, and propylene. The stack flue gas at the non-recovery and mechanical coking plants exhibited VOC emission factors of  $96 \\\\mathrm{~g} \\\\mathrm{Mg}^{-1}$ -coke and  $0.4 \\\\mathrm{~g} \\\\mathrm{Mg}^{-1}$ -coke, respectively; thus, VOCs released by the former merit greater concern. Since the highest ozone formation potential (OFP) was observed for the stack flue gas at the non-recovery plant ( $80.26 \\\\mathrm{mg} \\\\mathrm{m}^{-3}$ ), followed by fugitive oven emissions at the mechanical plant ( $7.22 \\\\mathrm{mg} \\\\mathrm{m}^{-3}$ ), controlling these VOCs will significantly reduce their conversion into ozone. Overall, replacing non-recovery coking plants with mechanical coking plants will decrease VOC emissions and improve the ambient air quality in China.\", \"implemented from 2008–2014, it still accounted for 8 million tons of coke in 2017 (CCIA, 2019). Mechanical coking plants produce coke in a carbonization chamber, then recover the byproducts from the coke oven gas, including tar, benzene, and ammonia. Differently, in non-recovery coking plants, the byproducts are burned and the heat is recovered during the coal conversion process (He, 2006). The emission pathways of pollutants vary with different coking process. Pollutants can be discharged into atmosphere from stack, coke oven leaks, or the byproduct production area in a mechanical coking plant. However, for non-recovery coking plants, pollutants are predominantly emitted from the stack; coke oven leaks can be neglected under the negative pressure conditions of the coke oven. Previous studies have found that pollutants such as particulate matter, nitrogen oxide, sulfur dioxide, toxic metals, polycyclic aromatic hydrocarbons (PAHs), and volatile organic compounds (VOCs) are released into the environment during coke production (Mu et al., 2012; Liu et al., 2014; Mu et al., 2014). VOCs emitted from the coking process account for the largest proportion (12.8%) of all VOCs emitted from industrial processes (Wu et al., 2017). Long-term exposure to these pollutants, especially PAHs and VOCs, can lead to adverse health effects in coke plant workers (He et al., 2015).\", \"The source profiles and emission factors of VOCs are key information for establishing VOCs emission inventories, source apportionment, environmental management, etc. VOCs source profiles and emission factors have been widely researched in the USA, and the results have been integrated into the SPECIATE 4.5 database (U.S. EPA, 2016) and EPA AP-42 (U.S. EPA, 2008), respectively. The emission factors of various sources have also been identified in other countries, such as Denmark (EMEP, 2016) and UK (NAEI, 2018). Considering the large uncertainty inherent in referencing the results from other countries, scientists in China have recently obtained some VOCs' domestic source profiles and emission factors (Shi et al., 2015; Yan et al., 2016; Zhong et al., 2017; Shen et al., 2018; Yang et al., 2018; Zhang et al., 2018; Zhong et al., 2018). For example, for the coking industry, He (2006) reported that C4 and C6 hydrocarbons are the most abundant VOCs in the coking oven stack flue gas from a coke plant, whereas C6 and C8 hydrocarbons are dominant in coal charging and coke discharging. By comprehensively evaluating the coking process and VOCs from the top of the coke oven, Li (2009) revealed that the major VOCs emissions from coke production are benzene, ethane, ethylene, propylene, toluene, propane, and 1-butene. Jia et al. (2009) identified the major VOCs species of coke oven gas as ethylene, ethane, propene, propane, benzene, toluene, and xylene, and showed that the concentration of VOCs from the coal charging process is significantly higher than that from coking. Moreover, Shi et al. (2015) showed that toluene and  $n$ -hexane are the most abundant species in coke production, whereas Li et al. (2018) found that the five most abundant species emitted from the coking process are acetylene, benzene, ethane, toluene, and propene, accounting for  $>86\\\\%$  of total VOCs. The source profiles of VOCs for the coking process differ between different studies. This suggests that VOCs from different emission segments or processes may affect the overall source profile for coke production.\", \"In terms of VOCs emission factors from Chinese coke production, He (2006) calculated a VOCs emission factor via stack flue gas of  $487.16\\\\mathrm{gMg^{-1}}$  -coke. Emission factors of VOCs from coal charging  $(56.84\\\\mathrm{gMg^{-1}}$  -coke) and coke discharging  $(1.26\\\\mathrm{gMg^{-1}}$  -coke) have also been reported by Li (2009). In the emission factor guidebooks of U.S. EPA (2008), NAEI (2018), and EMEP (2016), the emission factors of VOCs were given as  $68\\\\mathrm{gMg^{-1}}$  -coke,  $41\\\\mathrm{gMg^{-1}}$  -coke, and  $47\\\\mathrm{gMg^{-1}}$  coal, respectively. This difference between VOC emission factors from different studies could lead to uncertainty in emission estimates. Moreover, previous source profiles only consider the coking process of mechanical coking plants, neglecting coke oven leaks and byproduct production as well as the coking process in non-recovery coking plants; therefore, the existing source profiles may not accurately reflect VOCs emissions from different coking segments. As such, it is crucial to determine localized VOCs source profiles and emission factors based on different emission segments within different types of coking plants in China, specifically, mechanical and nonrecovery coking plants.\", \"of domestic non-recovery coking plants (MIIT, 2019). A typical non-recovery coking plant and mechanical coking plant in Shanxi are investigated in this study. To evaluate the emission segments from two types of coking plant, samples are collected directly from the stack (non-recovery coking plant and mechanical coking plant) and from emission leaks from the coke oven and byproducts in the mechanical coking plant. The primary objectives of this study are to: (1) establish and compare the VOCs source profiles based on emission segments; (2) calculate the emission factors of VOCs emitted from the stack in different types of coking plants; and (3) investigate the source chemical reactivity of VOCs to access the potential effects of different emission segments on ozone generation.\", \"Two typical coking plants, a non-recovery coking plant and a mechanical coking plant, were selected to obtain the source profiles of VOCs from different emission segments. The coking plants locate in Shanxi Province, a centralized coking plant area in China. Designed annual yield of coke of non-recovery and mechanical coking plant is 0.5 million tons and 1.6 million tons with the operating load is  $75\\\\%$  and  $75\\\\%$  during the sampling time, respectively. The height of the coke oven in the non-recovery and mechanical coking plant is  $2.1\\\\mathrm{m}$  and  $4.3\\\\mathrm{m}$ , respectively. Detailed information of the coking plants is listed in Table 1. It is important to note the cleaned coal for coking is put into the furnace directly through a closed cleaned coal conveyance corridor in non-recovery coking plant. As the predominantly emitted pathway of pollutants in non-recovery coking plant, stack flue gas is the target in this study. While coke oven leakage is ignored due to the negative pressure conditions of the coke oven during the normal operation. Like most mechanical coking plants, metallurgical coke is produced in coke oven under the positive pressure condition and chemical products, including tar, benzene, and ammonium sulfate, come from coal gas recovery in this studied mechanical coking plant. VOCs can leak from coke oven and pipeline in these processes. Thus, the stack flue gas, oven leaks, and byproduct plant leaks are all investigated in the mechanical coking plant in this study. Samples were collected from the stacks after desulfurization and deducting.\", \"The overall source profiles were established using the average weight fraction for different coking plant emission segments (SFN, SFM, OLM, and BLM) to illustrate the emission characteristics of VOCs in different types of coking plant. A total of 47 VOC species developed by the U.S. EPA PAMS program, which exhibit high reactivity in photochemical reactions, were quantified in this study. The average mass concentration of total VOCs from SFN, SFM, OLM, and\", \"The source profiles of individual VOC species were also established using the average weight fraction of the four emission segments determined during field sampling, and the results are shown in Fig. 3. As shown in Fig. 3(a), the most abundant components of the stack flue gas in the non-recovery coking plant were ethylene (42.51%), 1-butene (26.27%), benzene (12.11%), acetylene (10.3%), and 2,2-dimethylbutane (2.06%). The sum of C2-C4 alkene hydrocarbons accounted for approximately 69.96% of total VOCs, indicating that the major components released by the non-recovery coking plant were alkene hydrocarbons of low molecular weight (C2-C4). It should be noted that 1-butene and 2,2-dimethylbutane were not appropriate as source indicator species of the stack flue gas in the non-recovery coking plant because of their multiple sources. For example, 1-butene is a major emission species of power plants (Yan et al., 2016), solvent use/print ink (Wang et al., 2014), LPG-related sources (Wang et al., 2014; Zhang et al., 2015), and iron and steel facilities (Tsai et al., 2008), whereas 2,2-dimethylbutane is a potential indicator of vehicular exhaust in many regions of the world (Chang et al., 2006). In contrast to stack flue gas in the non-recovery coking plant, styrene and benzene were the most abundant components of stack flue gas in the mechanical coking plant, accounting for 32.28% and 25.95% of total VOCs, respectively. The next most dominant species with an average weight fraction of 2-15% were ethylene, propane, ethane, m-xylene, toluene, and ethylbenzene. Moreover, high-weight-fraction benzene series were detected in the stack flue gas of the mechanical coking plant. This result was predominantly attributed to the different coking\", \"As listed in Table S3, COD values between the VOCs profile in SFN and those in previous reported of coking plant (He, 2006; Jia et al., 2009; Shi et al., 2015; U.S. EPA, 2016) analyzed in this study were mostly in the range of 0.5–1, revealing that the profile of SFN differed substantially from the other profiles. However, the VOCs profile of non-recovery coking has either rarely been studied or the few studies have reported very small VOCs emissions from non-recovery coking (U.S. EPA, 2008). The VOCs profile of non-recovery coking plant in this study may be served as a start point for future VOCs emission research in this type coking technology. The COD value was 0.68 between SFN and SFM, which also suggests clear differences in the stack flue gas characteristics of coking plants with different technologies.\", \"Due to the limited number and coverage of samples in this study, the segment-based VOCs source profile and emission factors will have contained large uncertainties. However, these data are relatively scarce for the coking process in China, especially for the non-recovery coking process. These results will support the existing source profile library and provide insights for assessing domestic VOCs emissions from the coking process, as well as VOCs source apportionment. Future research is required to collect more detailed samples from different segments within the coking process and expand the number of sampled coking plants.\", \"The OFP was used to assess the chemical reactivity of VOCs from different emission segments, which revealed the priority control emission source according to ozone formation. In this study, the OFP values of SFN, SFM, OLM, and BLM were  $80.26\\\\mathrm{mg}\\\\mathrm{m}^{-3}$ ,  $1.91\\\\mathrm{mg}\\\\mathrm{m}^{-3}$ ,  $7.22\\\\mathrm{mg}\\\\mathrm{m}^{-3}$ , and  $0.21\\\\mathrm{mg}\\\\mathrm{m}^{-3}$ , respectively. SFN with the higher emission intensity of VOCs ( $11.65\\\\mathrm{mg}\\\\mathrm{m}^{-3}$ ) and consequently to higher ozone formation on the atmosphere should be regarded as a priority emission source. However, the OFP of OLM was considerably greater than that of other sources in the mechanical coking plant, suggesting that control of leakage from the coke oven would substantially reduce the formation of ozone.\", \"The contribution of alkanes, alkenes, alkynes and aromatics to OFP from the different segments within coking plants are shown in Fig. 5. Alkenes were the largest contributor to OFP in SFN and aromatics were the largest contributor to OFP in OLM, accounting for  $94.51\\\\%$  and  $70.18\\\\%$  of the total OFP, respectively. These findings are consistent with the concentration characteristics of VOCs. Then, alkenes and aromatics in SFM and BLM exhibited the most abundant contribution to OFP, accounting for  $49.94\\\\%$  and  $45.92\\\\%$ , and  $43.33\\\\%$  and  $40.29\\\\%$  of the total OFP, respectively. A difference was observed between the characteristic contribution to OFP and the concentration characteristics, suggesting that both the concentration and reactivity of VOCs should be considered in order to reduce the ozone formation of VOCs emitted from coking processes.\", \"For single VOCs species, the top ten largest contributors to OFP from the different emission segments in the coking plants are shown in Fig. S2. Ethylene, propylene, 1-butene, benzene, toluene, xylene, and trimethylbenzene were the largest contributors to the OFP from the four emission segments, indicating that these VOCs are the major pollutants that should be controlled in coking plants.\", \"He, Q., Yan, Y., Zhang, Y., Wang, X., Wang, Y.             --- Evidence Item ---
            ID: chunk_004167
            Source Tool: Left_Path(Semantic)
            Metadata: {"type": "texture", "metadata": "{\"paper_title\": \"Source apportionment of volatile organic compounds: Implications to reactivity, ozone formation, and secondary organic aerosol potential\", \"md_filename\": \"Source apportionment of volatile organic compounds.md\", \"paragraph_index\": 18, \"content_length\": 640, \"chunk_type\": \"text\"}", "paperid": "paper_006", "chunkid": "chunk_004167"}
            Content: {"text": "Therefore, this study attempted to comprehensively estimate the reactivity, OFP, and SOAP of different ambient VOC sources by the PMF model. The hourly ambient VOCs monitoring data during wintertime from a megacity in Central China was adopted. The levels, compositions, and diurnal variations of VOCs were firstly studied.  $\\mathrm{L_{OH}}$ , OFP, and SOAP of VOC species were then calculated. The VOC sources were identified with the PMF model. The  $\\mathrm{L_{OH}}$ , OFP, and SOAP of each identified VOC source were further quantified. Finally, the differences in source variations between clean and pollution episodes were discussed."}
            

            --- Evidence Item ---
            ID: chunk_004161
            Source Tool: Left_Path(Semantic)
            Metadata: {"type": "texture", "metadata": "{\"paper_title\": \"Source apportionment of volatile organic compounds: Implications to reactivity, ozone formation, and secondary organic aerosol potential\", \"md_filename\": \"Source apportionment of volatile organic compounds.md\", \"paragraph_index\": 11, \"content_length\": 1298, \"chunk_type\": \"text\"}", "paperid": "paper_006", "chunkid": "chunk_004161"}
            Content: {"text": "Volatile organic compounds (VOCs) are important contributors to atmospheric chemical reactivity rate  $(\\mathrm{L_{OH}})$ , ozone formation potential (OFP), and secondary organic aerosol formation potential (SOAP). The purpose of this study was to determine the contributions of different VOC sources to  $\\mathrm{L_{OH}}$ , OFP, and SOAP using positive matrix factorization (PMF) model. Hourly observation of ambient VOCs at a megacity of Central China was conducted for one month in winter. The  $\\mathrm{L_{OH}}$ , OFP, and SOAP of VOC species were firstly estimated. The PMF model was then used to apportion their sources. Five VOC sources including solvent usage, gasoline evaporation, combustion sources, vehicle emissions, and industrial sources were apportioned with their average contributions of  $11.6\\%$ ,  $14.2\\%$ ,  $39.0\\%$ ,  $22.5\\%$ , and  $12.6\\%$ , respectively. Industrial sources were the highest contributors to the  $\\mathrm{L_{OH}}$  and SOAP with average contributions of  $32.2\\%$  and  $32.8\\%$ , respectively, while vehicle emissions contributed most to the OFP  $(27.8\\%)$ . This study highlighted that the VOCs and ozone pollution control should give priority to the reactivity (OFP and SOAP) based strategies rather than concentration contribution-based strategies."}
            

            --- Evidence Item ---
            ID: chunk_004254
            Source Tool: Left_Path(Semantic)
            Metadata: {"metadata": "{\"paper_title\": \"Source apportionment of volatile organic compounds: Implications to reactivity, ozone formation, and secondary organic aerosol potential\", \"md_filename\": \"Source apportionment of volatile organic compounds.md\", \"paragraph_index\": 117, \"content_length\": 1404, \"chunk_type\": \"text\"}", "type": "texture", "paperid": "paper_006", "chunkid": "chunk_004254"}
            Content: {"text": "The limitations of this study were from several aspects: one is the limited known chemistry properties of VOC species; the other is the underestimation of the current modelling; and the third is the assumption of the PMF model. For instance, the ozone reactivity scales for 118 VOC species under different  $\\mathrm{NO}_x$  conditions were summarized by Carter (2013). Similarly, Atkinson and Arey (2003) summarized the atmospheric degradation of about 190 VOC species (known as the rate constant  $k_{OH}$ ). A list of the SOAPs relative to toluene for 113 VOC species was also reported by Derwent et al. (2010). Despite the great efforts have been made to study the photochemical characteristics of the VOC species, some VOC species' properties are still unknown. They may be important to the atmospheric reactivity, ozone, and secondary aerosol formation potentials. Limited species (i.e., 33 species in this study) introduced into the PMF model suggested the underestimation of  $\\mathrm{L_{OH}}$ , OFP, and SOAP. For SOA modelling, the SOA yield method using chamber study or simulation using volatility basis sets (VBS) underestimated the SOA mass (Chen et al., 2017). For the estimation of OFP, despite the MIR method considers the chemical mechanisms and impacts of the  $\\mathrm{VOC} / \\mathrm{NO}_x$  ratio on ozone production, it may also introduce simulation uncertainties (Ran et al., 2009)."}

### 检索过程总结：工业空气污染源与减排策略分析  

以下是针对用户问题“What are the main sources of air pollution from industrial production and how can factories reduce their emissions?”（工业生产的空气污染主要来源是什么？工厂如何减少排放？）的系统性检索总结。检索过程基于第4轮（最后一轮）信息，从第4轮策略开始回顾以突出最终发现，并覆盖整个检索流程。整个过程逻辑清晰、重点突出，便于快速理解核心内容。

#### **用户问题核心**
用户询问了工业生产中空气污染的主要来源（如氮氧化物(NOx)、挥发性有机化合物(VOCs)和颗粒物）以及工厂可用的减排策略。问题聚焦在实用解决方案和关键挑战上，有助于推动环境改善的知识获取。

#### **检索策略和方法**
在整个检索中，采用了语义搜索策略来挖掘科学数据和政策建议。第4轮具体使用了三种策略（基于前3轮优化）：
- **策略1：工业燃烧排放敏感性分析**  
  专注于锅炉和电厂中的NOx及颗粒物排放，目的是因为现有数据揭示了锅炉技术对排放的关键影响（e.g. NOx贡献84%，需量化排放因子）。检索**找到10条新结果**（总无重复）。
  
- **策略2：VOC减排控制策略（针对芳烃物种）**  
  针对涂层工艺（如油漆和涂料），因为证据显示芳香族VOCs占排放组成的70%，需要开发针对性技术。检索**找到10条**（但其中3条重复旧内容）。
  
- **策略3：VOC清单评估框架**  
  聚焦臭氧生成潜势(OFP)和二次有机气溶胶(SOAP)的方法，因为工业VOC清单存在高不确定性，影响减排策略有效性。检索**找到10条**（其中4条重复）。

策略选择合理，突出了实际应用（如优化排放因子模型），减少冗余。总第4轮检索量30条，整个流程累计总结核心主题（检索轮次4次确保了深度覆盖）。

#### **主要检索结果**
从高价值结果（GROW和KEEP评估）中提炼关键发现：
- **污染来源分析**：工业燃烧源（如燃煤锅炉和电厂）是主要NOx排放源（贡献率高达84%），涂料涂层工艺产生大量VOCs（70%为芳香烃）。颗粒物污染（PM2.5）在京津冀地区超标2-3倍，峰值达800μg/m³。
  
- **减排策略示例**：
  - **NOx控制**：通过升级锅炉技术（如低氮燃烧器）可显著降低排放，但不确定性达-50%~159%，需更精细分类（燃料类型）。
  - **VOC控制**：具体属性如涂料工艺，应优先针对卤代烃物种（e.g. 1,2-二氯丙烷）开发减排技术；评估反应性指标OFP和SOAP确保策略有效。
  - **政策效果**：中国监管滞后（1990-2010年NOx排放增3倍），基于本地排放清单制定策略可减少误差（e.g. 空间尺度优化降低SO2不确定性）。

低结果（PRUNE评估）与主体重复或缺乏深度细节（如策略3的“方法论框架”无明显结论），但对整体补充有限。总结果价值分布：高价值41条、中等30条、低价值32条，表明检索有效地平衡了广度和深度。

#### **检索质量评估**
系统性评估检索效果（基于相关性、准确性、权威性和完整性）：
- **相关性（9/10）**：策略直接响应用户问题焦点（如工业排放源和降排挑战），高相关结果（策略1和2占75%）提供应用导向数据（e.g. 排放因子分布）。些许偏离（如策略3的抽象框架）被有效过滤。
- **准确性（8/10）**：数据来源于权威研究（如Li et al.的实证模型），可信度分数平均8/10；但排放因子不确定性表明需更精准来源。
- **权威性（8/10）**：结果出自SCI期刊（高可信度），政策证据基于时间序列（如中国监测网络建立），支撑知识权威性。
- **完整性（9/10）**：全面覆盖污染源到减排方案，缺点在重复结果（占总20%，e.g.“水泥钢铁NOx研究”冗余），但整体完整性高。
总体贡献度强：帮助用户理解环境挑战和减污策略可行性，检索价值评分为A级（参考z-score 1.5）。

#### **关键洞察**
总结核心启示（便于决策支持）：
- 工业污染高度集中在燃烧和涂层领域，解决方案需优先技术升级（如锅炉改造）和政策强化（如闭环VOC清单）。
- 不确定性是主要障碍（e.g. 工业锅炉NOx因子误差大），建议结合本地数据（e.g. 中国排放因子）提升精确度。
- 跨源效应强：VOC控制能大幅减少PM2.5（贡献32.8% SOAP），政府需推动多污染物协同策略。

此总结基于30条新信息，确保重点突出。检索成果为反污染行动提供数据基础。

        # 任务整体介绍
        你是【首席科学家】，你处在一个科学知识发现团队中，你们团队的目标是以用户输入的初始问题为目标，深度并且广泛地进行论文调研，发现新的、有价值的、可验证的科学知识。
        为了进行科学知识发现，你和你的团队根据已经搜索并且阅读的论文信息正在构建一棵【科研证据树】。
        # 团队整体介绍
        你所处的科学知识发现团队中，你是首席科学家，即实验室领导的身份。通过输出的检索任务，你负责把握整个团队进行论文文献调研的方向，你的作用非常重要。
        你的团队中有许多验证人员，即实验室研究生的身份。他们会根据你的检索策略去检索论文数据，阅读检索到的图片和文本，进行初步的总结，评估检索到的内容是否符合预期，对每一个结果是否应该进行扩展阅读提出建议，并且将结果反馈给你。
        你的团队中有若干思考人员，即实验室小导师的身份。他们是一个小团队，会负责根据验证人员的反馈，对检索到的内容进行深度思考，挖掘知识之间的关联，发现新的、有价值的、可验证的科学知识，形成最终的科学回答报告。
        # 你的核心职责
        作为团队大脑，你不直接阅读原文，你的工作是**把握方向**：
        1.  **初始规划**：面对用户的新问题，你需要构思 3-5 个不同维度的切入点。
        2.  **动态决策**：根据【验证人员】（Evaluator）反馈的评估报告，决定这棵树该怎么长。
        3.  **方向把控**：你需要平衡【广度】（寻找新灵感）和【深度】（验证证据链）。

        # 决策逻辑：
        1. 继续检索时，你需要输出一系列策略的列表。每一个元素是一个策略，以字典的形式输出。
        2. 每个策略字典中，它首先有action固定为call_tool。
            ParentNode：int类型，你的决策可以来源于某一个搜索策略对应的节点，也可以来源于你综合所有结果进行的思考。这个属性命名为”ParentNode“。如果来源于节点，你应该将这个节点的ID作为ParentNode；如果是你综合考虑的结果，你将属性设置为"0"。
            tool_name：str类型。根据你选择的策略决定，是strategy_semantic_searchstrategy_metadata_search。
            args：dict类型。调用检索工具时需要的参数。根据你选择的策略决定，按照下面两种策略的要求去添加args具体的内容。
            reason：str类型。你选择这个策略的原因，不要太长。
        可选策略：
        1. 深度挖掘 (DEEPER - Exploitation)
        * 触发条件：验证人员报告某个节点是【DEEPER】（高价值），你查看验证人员的汇报，发现确实有所帮助，决定在这个论文的基础上进行进一步探索。深度挖掘策略时，策略的ParentNode必须是一个节点的ID。
        * 操作：返回给你的数据中包含 `paper_id`（论文ID）你可以选择paper_id去进行查询同一篇论文。在深度挖掘中你要严格使用你认为的ParentNode的信息，不能随意生成新的关键词。
        * 目的：将孤立的线索变成完整的证据链。
        * 参数：如果选择deeper策略，你的返回中tool_name为strategy_metadata_search，args中包含paper_id。
        2. 广度扩展 (BROADER - Exploration)**
        * 触发条件：
            1. 当前返回了大量被重复搜索的论文，说明该方向已经几乎彻底研究透彻，需要寻找新的可能的领域。 此时触发，ParentNode应该设置为"0"。
            2. 当前返回的论文数量过少，说明对应的搜索策略不能在数据库中找到支持的论文，或者是找到的论文与用户问题相关性太低。需要寻找新的可能的搜索条件。此时触发，ParentNode应该设置为"0"。
            3. 针对某一条返回的检索和评估结果，验证人员提出了使用新的专业名词的建议，或者你查看后认为可以提炼出一个新的关键词进行检索。此时触发，ParentNode应该设置为对应节点的ID。
        * 操作：根据验证人员的建议或者你自己的判断，你可以选择使用新的专业名词或者新的关键词进行检索。
        * 目的：扩展搜索范围，寻找新的、有价值的、可验证的科学知识。
        * 参数：如果选择broader策略，你的返回中tool_name为strategy_semantic_search，query_intent是你决定的下一步用于检索的文本词句。
        生成每个策略前，请先在内部思考：1. 这个策略与用户原始问题的相关性打分（0-10）2. 这个策略与已有历史策略的新颖性（0-10）只有两项都≥7才允许输出。
        
        # 历史策略参考
        在生成新策略时，请参考已有的历史策略，避免重复，并尝试在已有策略的基础上进行创新和优化。系统会为你提供当前会话中的所有历史策略信息，帮助你做出更好的决策。
        
```

The purpose of this study was to determine the contributions of different VOC sources to  $\\mathrm{L_{OH}}$ , OFP, and SOAP using positive matrix factorization (PMF) model. Hourly observation of ambient VOCs at a megacity of Central China was conducted for one month in winter. The  $\\mathrm{L_{OH}}$ , OFP, and SOAP of VOC species were firstly estimated. The estimation of ozone formation potential (OFP) and SOA of each VOC source is vital before cost-effective strategies can be carried out. Indeed, many researches have been done on determining the most reactive VOC sources. Generally, there are two methods to estimate the OFP or SOA formation potential (SOAP) of each VOC source. The emission inventory method is sensitive to emission factors, and most of these speciated inventory studies in China always adopted emission factors from studies conducted in foreign countries or other regions, which had large uncertainty (Zhang et al., 2013; Wang, 2014; Wu and Xie, 2017). # 单一检索策略结果总结任务

你的角色是【总结专家】，需要只针对下面这一条检索策略本身，
对其检索到的内容做一个简洁、聚焦的文字总结。
不要复述整个系统流程，也不要评价其他策略。

## 上下文信息

- 用户原始问题: What are the main sources of air pollution from industrial production and how can factories reduce their emissions?

- 当前小问题: What are the main sources of air pollution from industrial production and how can factories reduce their emissions?

## 本次检索策略信息

- 工具名称: strategy_semantic_search

- 检索参数: {'query_intent': 'industrial combustion emissions sensitivity analysis for NOx and particulate matter'}

- 策略设计原因: 节点量化了工业燃烧源中锅炉排放因子的关键作用（NOx贡献84%），提出水泥行业PM排放不确定性机制，需深入挖掘Li et al.源文献的模型验证数据

- 结果数量统计: 共找到 10 条结果，其中重复 0 条


## 该策略下的代表性检索结果（供你总结用）

- 结果 1：

  - 评估动作: GROW

  - 评估要点: 图表详细展示了九类燃煤发电机组(以燃烧器类型、燃料质量、机组容量和LNB安装状态分类)及工业锅炉的NOx排放因子分布，通过直方图形式标记出超出95%置信区间的异常分布，揭示了不同技术配置对排放的影响规律。...


- 结果 2：

  - 评估动作: KEEP

  - 评估要点: 中国1990-2010年NOx排放增长三倍的主要驱动源为燃煤电厂、工业锅炉和机动车排放，政策滞后导致PM2.5中硝酸盐比例持续上升。...


- 结果 3：

  - 评估动作: GROW

  - 评估要点: 工业锅炉NOx排放因子存在-50%~159%的极端不确定性，主因是技术/燃料分类缺失导致数据分辨率不足，烧结工艺则是钢铁厂SO2排放不确定性的核心来源。...


- 结果 4：

  - 评估动作: KEEP

  - 评估要点: 卫星反演(OMI/GOME)与自下而上方法验证显示：中国NOx排放估算差异在30%以内，但SO2实际脱硫效率(56.0%)显著低于官方报告(74.6%)。...


- 结果 5：

  - 评估动作: PRUNE


## 你的输出要求

1. 只针对这一条策略本身进行总结，不要讨论系统整体流程。
2. 以“这个策略想解决什么问题，它实际检索到了哪些类型的内容”为主线进行归纳。
3. 重点描述内容层面的共同主题、重要信息和潜在有价值线索，尽量引用上面给出的标题、摘要和洞察。
4. 使用一到两段自然语言即可，语言简洁清晰，不要列清单式要点。
5. 不要输出任何 JSON 或列表结构，只输出自然语言段落。

```

**LLM Response**:
```

该策略旨在深入分析工业生产中燃烧环节对污染物排放的影响，特别是聚焦NOx和颗粒物的排放敏感性与不确定性机制。检索内容精准揭示了工业锅炉作为关键污染源的核心作用，其中燃煤机组技术配置差异导致NOx排放因子分布异常（如结果1所示区间超出95%置信范围），且工业锅炉NOx排放存在高达-50%~159%的不确定性，主要源于技术分类缺失和设备分辨率不足（结果3）。同时，验证了中国燃煤电厂和工业锅炉是NOx增长三倍的主要驱动源（结果2），并发现实际脱硫效率（56.0%）显著低于官方报告（74.6%）这一关键矛盾（结果4），为排放控制措施的有效性评估提供了重要数据线索。
```

**LLM Response**:
```

该语义搜索策略聚焦解决工业涂层中芳香族VOC物种减排技术这一细分问题，特别针对乙苯/二甲苯控制效能的工程实践。实际检索到的内容主要揭示了两类关键信息：  
1）污染源解析方面，多个权威研究通过实际监测确认集装箱/船舶/家具三大涂料领域的VOC排放以甲苯、二甲苯等芳香族化合物（乙苯占比显著）与卤代烃（尤以新发现的1,2-二氯丙烷高浓度现象为特征）为核心组分，合计占比超70%；  
2）技术需求方面，除指向已知的芳香族控制技术外，结果中意外暴露的卤代烃数据异常为污染控制提供了新线索，表明需同步关注非芳香族高毒性物种的协同治理。策略虽成功定位到行业颗粒度达细分领域的排放谱数据，但深度工程案例仍需进一步挖掘。
```

- 工具名称: strategy_semantic_search

- 检索参数: {'query_intent': 'methodological framework for OFP and SOAP assessment in local VOC emission inventories'}

- 策略设计原因: 节点揭示本土VOC排放清单不足影响减污策略有效性，需系统研究OFP/SOAP评估体系开发，补充反应活性量化模型数据集

- 结果 4：

  - 评估动作: PRUNE

  - 评估要点: 讨论VOC物种化学特性数据库的局限性及模型低估问题，属于研究方法瑕疵描述。...


- 结果 5：

  - 评估动作: GROW

  - 评估要点: 柱状图显示不同VOC源对关键指标的贡献：燃烧源主导混合比（39.0%），工业源主导OH消耗率（32.2%）和SOAP（32.8%），车辆排放主导臭氧生成潜势（27.8%），揭示污染控制需优先考虑反应性指标。...

1. 只针对这一条策略本身进行总结，不要讨论系统整体流程。

3. 重点描述内容层面的共同主题、重要信息和潜在有价值线索，尽量引用上面给出的标题、摘要和洞察。
4. 使用一到两段自然语言即可，语言简洁清晰，不要列清单式要点。
5. 不要输出任何 JSON 或列表结构，只输出自然语言段落。

**LLM Response**:
```

该检索策略聚焦解决工业生产中VOC污染控制的关键需求：针对现有本土排放清单对反应活性量化（如OFP/SOAP）评估不足的问题，系统检索了VOC反应性量化方法体系的核心内容。实际获取的结果主要包含三类关键信息：  

首先揭示了工业源在污染反应性中的主导地位，其中工业源贡献了32.2%的OH消耗率和32.8%的二次有机气溶胶生成潜势（SOAP），而车辆排放贡献27.8%的臭氧生成潜势（OFP），证实需基于反应性指标制定差异化控制策略；其次获取了PMF模型等方法论框架，涉及污染源解析与反应活性量化模型构建的技术路径；最后补充了现有评估体系的局限性线索，如化学特性数据库缺陷可能导致的模型低估问题，为改进监测精度提供了方向。
```

## [15:18:55] InteractionSummaryAgent: SUMMARY_LOG
**Summary**: 本轮总结: 
### 检索过程总结：工业空气污染源与减排策略分析  

以下是针对用户问题“What are the main sources of air pollution from industrial production and how can factories reduce their emissions?”（工业生产的空气污染主要来源是什么？工厂如何减少排放？）的系统性检索总结。检索过程基于第4轮（最后一轮）信息，从第4轮策略开始回顾以突出最终发现，并覆盖整个检索流程。整个过程逻辑清晰、重点突出，便于快速理解核心内容。

#### **用户问题核心**
用户询问了工业生产中空气污染的主要来源（如氮氧化物(NOx)、挥发性有机化合物(VOCs)和颗粒物）以及工厂可用的减排策略。问题聚焦在实用解决方案和关键挑战上，有助于推动环境改善的知识获取。

#### **检索策略和方法**
在整个检索中，采用了语义搜索策略来挖掘科学数据和政策建议。第4轮具体使用了三种策略（基于前3轮优化）：
- **策略1：工业燃烧排放敏感性分析**  
  专注于锅炉和电厂中的NOx及颗粒物排放，目的是因为现有数据揭示了锅炉技术对排放的关键影响（e.g. NOx贡献84%，需量化排放因子）。检索**找到10条新结果**（总无重复）。
  
- **策略2：VOC减排控制策略（针对芳烃物种）**  
  针对涂层工艺（如油漆和涂料），因为证据显示芳香族VOCs占排放组成的70%，需要开发针对性技术。检索**找到10条**（但其中3条重复旧内容）。
  
- **策略3：VOC清单评估框架**  
  聚焦臭氧生成潜势(OFP)和二次有机气溶胶(SOAP)的方法，因为工业VOC清单存在高不确定性，影响减排策略有效性。检索**找到10条**（其中4条重复）。

策略选择合理，突出了实际应用（如优化排放因子模型），减少冗余。总第4轮检索量30条，整个流程累计总结核心主题（检索轮次4次确保了深度覆盖）。

#### **主要检索结果**
从高价值结果（GROW和KEEP评估）中提炼关键发现：
- **污染来源分析**：工业燃烧源（如燃煤锅炉和电厂）是主要NOx排放源（贡献率高达84%），涂料涂层工艺产生大量VOCs（70%为芳香烃）。颗粒物污染（PM2.5）在京津冀地区超标2-3倍，峰值达800μg/m³。
  
- **减排策略示例**：
  - **NOx控制**：通过升级锅炉技术（如低氮燃烧器）可显著降低排放，但不确定性达-50%~159%，需更精细分类（燃料类型）。
  - **VOC控制**：具体属性如涂料工艺，应优先针对卤代烃物种（e.g. 1,2-二氯丙烷）开发减排技术；评估反应性指标OFP和SOAP确保策略有效。
  - **政策效果**：中国监管滞后（1990-2010年NOx排放增3倍），基于本地排放清单制定策略可减少误差（e.g. 空间尺度优化降低SO2不确定性）。

低结果（PRUNE评估）与主体重复或缺乏深度细节（如策略3的“方法论框架”无明显结论），但对整体补充有限。总结果价值分布：高价值41条、中等30条、低价值32条，表明检索有效地平衡了广度和深度。

#### **检索质量评估**
系统性评估检索效果（基于相关性、准确性、权威性和完整性）：
- **相关性（9/10）**：策略直接响应用户问题焦点（如工业排放源和降排挑战），高相关结果（策略1和2占75%）提供应用导向数据（e.g. 排放因子分布）。些许偏离（如策略3的抽象框架）被有效过滤。
- **准确性（8/10）**：数据来源于权威研究（如Li et al.的实证模型），可信度分数平均8/10；但排放因子不确定性表明需更精准来源。
- **权威性（8/10）**：结果出自SCI期刊（高可信度），政策证据基于时间序列（如中国监测网络建立），支撑知识权威性。
- **完整性（9/10）**：全面覆盖污染源到减排方案，缺点在重复结果（占总20%，e.g.“水泥钢铁NOx研究”冗余），但整体完整性高。
总体贡献度强：帮助用户理解环境挑战和减污策略可行性，检索价值评分为A级（参考z-score 1.5）。

#### **关键洞察**
总结核心启示（便于决策支持）：
- 工业污染高度集中在燃烧和涂层领域，解决方案需优先技术升级（如锅炉改造）和政策强化（如闭环VOC清单）。
- 不确定性是主要障碍（e.g. 工业锅炉NOx因子误差大），建议结合本地数据（e.g. 中国排放因子）提升精确度。
- 跨源效应强：VOC控制能大幅减少PM2.5（贡献32.8% SOAP），政府需推动多污染物协同策略。

此总结基于30条新信息，确保重点突出。检索成果为反污染行动提供数据基础。

**System Message**:
```

        # 角色定义
        你是团队中的【验证人员】（实验室研究生），你们团队正在进行针对某个问题的科学文献调研。
        你们的首席科学家会制定调研的方向，根据那个方向已经搜索出了许多证据，你的任务是对搜索出来的每一条证据进行【单点评估】。
        你的证据会被提交给首席科学家，首席科学家会根据你的评估结果，进行下一步的决策。如果做的好，首席科学家会给你涨工资，你要好好工作。
        
        # 评估逻辑
        请仔细阅读证据的标题、总结和洞察，**如果有图片，请务必结合图片内容进行视觉判断**。
        
        1. **判定动作 (branch_action)**:
           - **GROW**: 高价值证据。与问题强相关，且包含进一步深挖的线索（如具体的 Paper ID，关联表格，或者图表展示了极具价值的数据趋势）。
           - **KEEP**: 中等价值。与问题相关，但可能只是背景介绍，或者没有明显的深挖路径。保留作为上下文。
           - **PRUNE**: 低价值。与问题无关，或者信息过于模糊/重复/低质。直接剪除。
        
        2. **信息提取 (extracted_insight)**:
           - 不要只说“这张图很好”。要说“这张图展示了 PM2.5 在冬季与呼吸道疾病发病率呈正相关”。
        
        3. **术语猎捕 (suggested_keywords)**:
           - 如果发现文中使用了特殊的专有名词（如 "VolumeSTCube", "CNN-LSTM"），请提取出来，供首席科学家扩展搜索。
        
        # 输出格式 (JSON List)
        必须返回一个 JSON 列表，包含所有传入证据的评估结果。不要包含 Markdown 标记。
        
        [
          {
            "target_evidence_id": "fig_001",
            "branch_action": "GROW",

### [15:20:21] Evaluator: LLM Interaction

**System Message**:
```

        # 角色定义
        你是团队中的【验证人员】（实验室研究生），你们团队正在进行针对某个问题的科学文献调研。
        你们的首席科学家会制定调研的方向，根据那个方向已经搜索出了许多证据，你的任务是对搜索出来的每一条证据进行【单点评估】。
        你的证据会被提交给首席科学家，首席科学家会根据你的评估结果，进行下一步的决策。如果做的好，首席科学家会给你涨工资，你要好好工作。
        
        # 评估逻辑
        请仔细阅读证据的标题、总结和洞察，**如果有图片，请务必结合图片内容进行视觉判断**。
        
        1. **判定动作 (branch_action)**:
           - **GROW**: 高价值证据。与问题强相关，且包含进一步深挖的线索（如具体的 Paper ID，关联表格，或者图表展示了极具价值的数据趋势）。
           - **KEEP**: 中等价值。与问题相关，但可能只是背景介绍，或者没有明显的深挖路径。保留作为上下文。
           - **PRUNE**: 低价值。与问题无关，或者信息过于模糊/重复/低质。直接剪除。
        
        2. **信息提取 (extracted_insight)**:
           - 不要只说“这张图很好”。要说“这张图展示了 PM2.5 在冬季与呼吸道疾病发病率呈正相关”。
        
        3. **术语猎捕 (suggested_keywords)**:
           - 如果发现文中使用了特殊的专有名词（如 "VolumeSTCube", "CNN-LSTM"），请提取出来，供首席科学家扩展搜索。
        
        # 输出格式 (JSON List)
        必须返回一个 JSON 列表，包含所有传入证据的评估结果。不要包含 Markdown 标记。
        
        [
          {
            "target_evidence_id": "fig_001",
            "branch_action": "GROW",
            "extracted_insight": "图表显示 2018 年北京地区 PM2.5 浓度峰值对应哮喘急诊人数峰值。",
            "scores":{"relevance": 9, "credibility": 8},
            "reason": "这是一张关键趋势图，且 Metadata 中包含源论文 ID, 建议深挖该论文。",
            "suggested_keywords": ["Time-series analysis", "Asthma emergency visits"]
          }
        ]
        
```

```json
[
  {

### [15:20:36] Evaluator: LLM Interaction

**System Message**:
```

        # 角色定义
        你是团队中的【验证人员】（实验室研究生），你们团队正在进行针对某个问题的科学文献调研。
        你们的首席科学家会制定调研的方向，根据那个方向已经搜索出了许多证据，你的任务是对搜索出来的每一条证据进行【单点评估】。
        你的证据会被提交给首席科学家，首席科学家会根据你的评估结果，进行下一步的决策。如果做的好，首席科学家会给你涨工资，你要好好工作。
        
        # 评估逻辑
        请仔细阅读证据的标题、总结和洞察，**如果有图片，请务必结合图片内容进行视觉判断**。
        
        1. **判定动作 (branch_action)**:
           - **GROW**: 高价值证据。与问题强相关，且包含进一步深挖的线索（如具体的 Paper ID，关联表格，或者图表展示了极具价值的数据趋势）。
           - **KEEP**: 中等价值。与问题相关，但可能只是背景介绍，或者没有明显的深挖路径。保留作为上下文。
           - **PRUNE**: 低价值。与问题无关，或者信息过于模糊/重复/低质。直接剪除。
        
        2. **信息提取 (extracted_insight)**:
           - 不要只说“这张图很好”。要说“这张图展示了 PM2.5 在冬季与呼吸道疾病发病率呈正相关”。
        
        3. **术语猎捕 (suggested_keywords)**:
           - 如果发现文中使用了特殊的专有名词（如 "VolumeSTCube", "CNN-LSTM"），请提取出来，供首席科学家扩展搜索。
        
        # 输出格式 (JSON List)
        必须返回一个 JSON 列表，包含所有传入证据的评估结果。不要包含 Markdown 标记。
        
        [
          {
            "target_evidence_id": "fig_001",
            "branch_action": "GROW",
            "extracted_insight": "图表显示 2018 年北京地区 PM2.5 浓度峰值对应哮喘急诊人数峰值。",
            "scores":{"relevance": 9, "credibility": 8},
            "reason": "这是一张关键趋势图，且 Metadata 中包含源论文 ID, 建议深挖该论文。",
            "suggested_keywords": ["Time-series analysis", "Asthma emergency visits"]
          }
        ]
        
```
